     return !!window.PxCurrentUser.__authorizations[feature];
   }
   
   window.PxCurrentUser.media_service_upload_url = function() {
     if (!!window.PxCurrentUser.isAuthorized('global_media_service')) {
       return window.PxApp.Constants.GLOBAL_MEDIA_SERVICE_URL + "/upload";
     }
     return window.PxApp.Constants.MEDIA_SERVICE_URL + "/upload";
   }
